# Changelog

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

## [0.1.62] - 2026-03-26

### Changed
- **OpenClaw reviewer** — Independent re-run **`2026-03-26T19:55:40Z`** (`HEAD` unchanged **`55dc6a8bb28d`**); prior **`2026-03-26T19:49:06Z`** / **`19:42:25Z`**; same checks (layout, `pnpm check` / `tsgo`, Vitest, §7 **Aligned**). (`005-openclaw-reviewer/005-openclaw-reviewer.md`.)

## [0.1.61] - 2026-03-26

### Added
- **Browser (CDP) & automation** — Proxy **Fetch** auth (`browserCdpProxyUsername` / `browserCdpProxyPassword`), **`browserCdpHttpTimeoutSecs`** / **`browserCdpWsConnectTimeoutSecs`**, SSRF awareness when HTTP(S) proxy env vars are set (`strictSsrfRejectWhenProxyEnv`), configurable Chromium port/binary/user-data-dir, vendored **`headless_chrome`** patch (`Tab::reset_fetch_auth_challenge_response_to_default`). CDP downloads, trace archive, cookie storage, DOM snapshot, screenshot annotation, URL filter, target-crash listener, permissions helper, artifact limits, **`browser_doctor`**, **`circuit_breaker`**; deps **`totp-rs`**, **`tungstenite`**, **`sha2`**, **`image`** / **`imageproc`** / **`ab_glyph`**.
- **Ollama, Discord, scheduler** — **`ollama_queue`**, model list cache, log **redaction**, run-error metrics, modular tool/command pipeline (registry, turn/ori lifecycle, outbound pipeline, session limits, compaction hooks, context assembler, untrusted content, LLM screenshot lifecycle, etc.). Discord/session-memory **before-reset** JSONL + optional shell hook; scheduler **heartbeat**; **`feature_health`** and dashboard/docs (**`docs/040_feature_health_dashboard.md`**). Dashboard / **`ollama.js`** updates.

### Changed
- **`BROWSER_SCROLL`** (viewport-based steps), **`BROWSER_EXTRACT`** (markdown from DOM), post-launch **`/json/version`** polling; expanded **`config.json`** and agent prompts; documentation refresh across browser, agents, memory, and logging references.
- **OpenClaw reviewer** — Independent re-run **`2026-03-26T19:17:34Z`** (`src/` layout, `pnpm check` chain (`format:check` → `pnpm tsgo`, no `"tsgo"` script key; `@typescript/native-preview` `7.0.0-dev.20260322.1`), Vitest thresholds/extends, §7 table; prior **`19:11:15Z`** / **`19:03:33Z`** / **`18:57:15Z`** / **`18:45:18Z`** / **`18:38:42Z`** / **`18:32:27Z`** / **`18:15:58Z`** / **`18:04:40Z`** / **`17:53:24Z`** / **`17:46:27Z`** / **`17:39:54Z`** / **`17:33:24Z`** / **`17:21:58Z`** / **`17:15:49Z`** / **`17:09:23Z`** / **`16:57:41Z`** / **`16:50:36Z`** / **`16:43:58Z`** / **`16:37:25Z`** / **`16:30:55Z`** / **`16:24:14Z`** / **`16:17:10Z`** / **`16:10:41Z`** / **`16:04:04Z`** / **`15:57:50Z`** / **`15:50:38Z`** / **`15:43:47Z`** / **`15:37:05Z`** / **`15:30:51Z`** / **`15:24:04Z`** / **`15:17:26Z`** / **`15:10:42Z`** / **`15:00:46Z`** / **`14:47:40Z`** / **`14:40:51Z`** / **`14:34:00Z`** / **`14:26:28Z`** / **`14:19:57Z`** / **`14:13:14Z`** / **`14:01:41Z`** / **`13:39:59Z`** / **`13:08:07Z`** / **`12:59:14Z`** / **`12:47:17Z`** / **`12:40:16Z`** / **`12:28:23Z`** / **`12:17:14Z`** / **`12:05:53Z`** / **`11:59:31Z`** / **`11:52:42Z`** / **`11:46:35Z`** / **`10:31:18Z`** archived); `HEAD` unchanged **`55dc6a8bb28d`** (full hash in reviewer doc); upstream status last check updated (**Aligned**). (`005-openclaw-reviewer/005-openclaw-reviewer.md`.)

## [0.1.60] - 2026-03-25

### Added
- **Browser agent (CDP)** — `browser_agent/cdp_url.rs`: derive HTTP(S) bases from `ws`/`wss` and debugger URLs (strip `/devtools/browser/…`, trailing `/cdp` for `/json/*`), rewrite loopback when the debugger advertises `0.0.0.0` or IPv6 unspecified, and **`redact_cdp_url`** for logs/errors; wired into `/json/version` discovery and WebSocket connect strings; unit tests. (`browser_agent/mod.rs`, `docs/029_browser_automation.md`.)
- **Scheduler → Discord delivery awareness** — After a successful scheduler post to Discord, append a bounded JSON log (`scheduler_delivery_awareness.json`), inject a short **recent-deliveries** block into the **CPU window / dashboard** Ollama system prompt, and list entries in Settings via **`list_scheduler_delivery_awareness`**. (`scheduler/delivery_awareness.rs`, `scheduler/mod.rs`, `discord/mod.rs`, `commands/ollama_frontend_chat.rs`, `commands/scheduler.rs`, `lib.rs`, `dashboard.html`, `dashboard.js`; `docs/009_scheduler_agent.md`, `docs/007_discord_agent.md`.)
- **Unix single-instance guard** — Optional fail-fast second launch using a non-blocking **`flock`** on `~/.mac-stats/single-instance.lock` (warn + exit 0 if another instance holds the lock). (`lib.rs`.)
- **Outbound Discord attachment roots** — `security/attachment_roots.rs` centralizes allowlisting: canonical roots under **`~/.mac-stats`** for screenshots, PDF exports, and browser downloads, plus optional **`extraAttachmentRoots`** in `config.json` (must resolve under `$HOME` or `~/.mac-stats`). Discord attachment sending filters through **`is_allowed_outbound_attachment_path`**. (`discord/mod.rs`, `config/mod.rs`, `security/mod.rs`, `docs/data_files_reference.md`.)
- **RUN_CMD pipeline hardening** — Each pipeline **stage** runs via `sh -c`; stages split **only** at top-level `|`. Quote-aware validation rejects `;`, `&&`, `||`, nested `|`, leading subshells, `$(…)`, backticks, process substitution, and stray background `&`; first token cannot be a nested shell/env wrapper (`bash`, `env`, …). (`commands/run_cmd.rs`, `docs/011_local_cmd_agent.md`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` extended with **`wave function(s)`**, **`slater determinant(s)`**, **`configuration state function(s)`**, **`csf coefficient(s)`**, **`ci coefficient(s)`**, **`mo coefficient(s)`**, **`natural orbital(s)`**, **`occupied orbital(s)`**, and **`canonical orbital(s)`** exceed / exceeded chains aligned with the existing context-slot pairing rules (FEAT-D458–D465, FEAT-D467). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)

### Changed
- **Browser agent (CDP)** — Trailing `/cdp` path normalization uses `strip_suffix("/cdp")` (clearer than manual slicing); empty path and bare `cdp` still normalize to `/`. (`browser_agent/cdp_url.rs`.)
- **Browser tools** — Dispatch and agent prompt tweaks alongside CDP wiring; **`BROWSER_EXTRACT`** CDP-fallback errors pass the message directly into `append_browser_readiness_context` (drop redundant `format!` wrapper). (`commands/browser_tool_dispatch.rs`, `commands/agent_descriptions.rs`.)
- **Browser session** — `BrowserSessionCell` type alias for the cached session `Mutex` (keeps `type_complexity` lint clean). (`browser_agent/mod.rs`.)
- **Single-instance lock** — Open `~/.mac-stats/single-instance.lock` with **`truncate(true)`** so stale contents are not retained across launches. (`lib.rs`.)
- **Task runner** — Minor review/runner integration. (`task/review.rs`, `task/runner.rs`.)
- **Docs & agent workflow** — OpenClaw reviewer / FEATURE-CODER verification timestamps, OpenClaw `HEAD`, and backlog through **FEAT-D467** / **FEAT-D466** (`005-openclaw-reviewer/005-openclaw-reviewer.md`, `006-feature-coder/FEATURE-CODER.md`); agent flow and automation references (`docs/020_agent_task_flow_analysis.md`, `docs/029_browser_automation.md`, etc.).

## [0.1.59] - 2026-03-25

### Added
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`atomic orbitals exceed`** / **`atomic orbitals exceeded`** and singular **`atomic orbital exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`molecular orbital exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`molecular orbitals exceed`**, so batch / JSON / DFT / quantum-chemistry-style APIs that describe request **`atomic orbitals`** (AO / valence counts) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`atomic`** so **`subatomic orbital exceed`**, **`preatomicorbital exceed`**, **`reatomicorbital exceed`**, and embedded **`atomic orbital exceed`** inside **`superatomicorbital exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`atomicorbitals`**, so the contiguous phrase **`atomic orbitals exceed`** is absent in **`microatomicorbitals exceed`** / **`metaatomicorbitals exceed`**; a spaced **`micro atomic orbitals …`** still matches at the boundary before **`atomic`**). Spaced **`micro atomic orbitals …`** with a slot is intentionally covered by the existing generic **`orbitals exceed`** arm. HTTP rate limits, AO-basis / valence-shell caps, and other **`atomic orbitals exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D457.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`molecular orbitals exceed`** / **`molecular orbitals exceeded`** and singular **`molecular orbital exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`density matrix exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`density matrices exceed`**, so batch / JSON / DFT / quantum-chemistry-style APIs that describe request **`molecular orbitals`** (MO / active-space counts) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`molecular`** so **`submolecular orbital exceed`**, **`premolecularorbital exceed`**, **`remolecularorbital exceed`**, and embedded **`molecular orbital exceed`** inside **`supermolecularorbital exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`molecularorbitals`**, so the contiguous phrase **`molecular orbitals exceed`** is absent in **`micromolecularorbitals exceed`** / **`metamolecularorbitals exceed`**; a spaced **`micro molecular orbitals …`** still matches at the boundary before **`molecular`**). Spaced **`micromolecular orbitals …`** with a slot is intentionally covered by the existing generic **`orbitals exceed`** arm. HTTP rate limits, active-space / MO-basis caps, and other **`molecular orbitals exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D456.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`density matrices exceed`** / **`density matrices exceeded`** and singular **`density matrix exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`gaussian shell exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`gaussian shells exceed`**, so batch / JSON / DFT / quantum-chemistry-style APIs that describe request **`density matrices`** (1-RDM / response-density blocks) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`density`** so **`microdensity matrices exceed`**, **`metadensity matrices exceed`**, **`subdensity matrix exceed`**, **`predensity matrix exceed`**, **`redensity matrix exceed`**, and embedded **`density matrix exceed`** inside **`superdensity matrix exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`densitymatrices`**, so the contiguous phrase **`density matrices exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro density matrices …`** still matches at the boundary before **`density`**). HTTP rate limits, per-orbital / N-representability caps, and other **`density matrices exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D455.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`gaussian shells exceed`** / **`gaussian shells exceeded`** and singular **`gaussian shell exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`cartesian gaussian exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`cartesian gaussians exceed`**, so batch / JSON / quantum-chemistry or Gaussian-basis APIs that describe request **`gaussian shells`** (shell / angular-momentum blocks in a Gaussian basis) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`gaussian`** so **`microgaussian shells exceed`**, **`metagaussian shells exceed`**, **`subgaussian shell exceed`**, **`pregaussian shell exceed`**, **`regaussian shell exceed`**, and embedded **`gaussian shell exceed`** inside **`supergaussian shell exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`gaussianshells`**, so the contiguous phrase **`gaussian shells exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro gaussian shells …`** still matches at the boundary before **`gaussian`**). HTTP rate limits, per-angular-momentum / shell-block caps, and other **`gaussian shells exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D454.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`cartesian gaussians exceed`** / **`cartesian gaussians exceeded`** and singular **`cartesian gaussian exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`spherical gaussian exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`spherical gaussians exceed`**, so batch / JSON / quantum-chemistry or Gaussian-basis APIs that describe request **`cartesian gaussians`** (Cartesian / solid-harmonic GTO counts) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`cartesian`** so **`microcartesian gaussians exceed`**, **`metacartesian gaussians exceed`**, **`subcartesian gaussian exceed`**, **`precartesian gaussian exceed`**, **`recartesian gaussian exceed`**, and embedded **`cartesian gaussian exceed`** inside **`supercartesian gaussian exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`cartesiangaussians`**, so the contiguous phrase **`cartesian gaussians exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro cartesian gaussians …`** still matches at the boundary before **`cartesian`**). HTTP rate limits, per-center / Cartesian-GTO caps, and other **`cartesian gaussians exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D453.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`spherical gaussians exceed`** / **`spherical gaussians exceeded`** and singular **`spherical gaussian exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`contracted gaussian exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`contracted gaussians exceed`**, so batch / JSON / quantum-chemistry or Gaussian-basis APIs that describe request **`spherical gaussians`** (SGF / spherical-harmonic Gaussian counts) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`spherical`** so **`microspherical gaussians exceed`**, **`metaspherical gaussians exceed`**, **`subspherical gaussian exceed`**, **`prespherical gaussian exceed`**, **`respherical gaussian exceed`**, and embedded **`spherical gaussian exceed`** inside **`superspherical gaussian exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`sphericalgaussians`**, so the contiguous phrase **`spherical gaussians exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro spherical gaussians …`** still matches at the boundary before **`spherical`**). HTTP rate limits, per-shell / SGF-basis caps, and other **`spherical gaussians exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D452.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`contracted gaussians exceed`** / **`contracted gaussians exceeded`** and singular **`contracted gaussian exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`primitive gaussian exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`primitive gaussians exceed`**, so batch / JSON / quantum-chemistry or Gaussian-basis APIs that describe request **`contracted gaussians`** (CGF counts) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`contracted`** so **`microcontracted gaussians exceed`**, **`metacontracted gaussians exceed`**, **`subcontracted gaussian exceed`**, **`precontracted gaussian exceed`**, **`recontracted gaussian exceed`**, and embedded **`contracted gaussian exceed`** inside **`supercontracted gaussian exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`contractedgaussians`**, so the contiguous phrase **`contracted gaussians exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro contracted gaussians …`** still matches at the boundary before **`contracted`**). HTTP rate limits, per-shell / CGF-basis caps, and other **`contracted gaussians exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D451.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`primitive gaussians exceed`** / **`primitive gaussians exceeded`** and singular **`primitive gaussian exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`auxiliary function exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`auxiliary functions exceed`**, so batch / JSON / quantum-chemistry or Gaussian-basis APIs that describe request **`primitive gaussians`** (PGF counts) still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`primitive`** so **`microprimitive gaussians exceed`**, **`metaprimitive gaussians exceed`**, **`subprimitive gaussian exceed`**, **`preprimitive gaussian exceed`**, **`reprimitive gaussian exceed`**, and embedded **`primitive gaussian exceed`** inside **`superprimitive gaussian exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`primitivegaussians`**, so the contiguous phrase **`primitive gaussians exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro primitive gaussians …`** still matches at the boundary before **`primitive`**). HTTP rate limits, per-shell / PGF-basis caps, and other **`primitive gaussians exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D450.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`auxiliary functions exceed`** / **`auxiliary functions exceeded`** and singular **`auxiliary function exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`basis function exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`basis functions exceed`**, so batch / JSON / DFT / density-fitting or RI-JK-style APIs that describe request **`auxiliary functions`** still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`auxiliary`** so **`microauxiliary functions exceed`**, **`metaauxiliary functions exceed`**, **`subauxiliary function exceed`**, **`preauxiliary function exceed`**, **`reauxiliary function exceed`**, and embedded **`auxiliary function exceed`** inside **`superauxiliary function exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`auxiliaryfunctions`**, so the contiguous phrase **`auxiliary functions exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro auxiliary functions …`** still matches at the boundary before **`auxiliary`**). - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`electrons exceed`** / **`electrons exceeded`** and singular **`electron exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`basis function exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`basis functions exceed`**, so batch / JSON / DFT / quantum-chemistry-style APIs that describe request **`electrons`** still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`electrons`** / **`electron`** so **`microelectrons exceed`**, **`metaelectrons exceed`**, **`subelectron exceed`**, **`preelectron exceed`**, **`reelectron exceed`**, and embedded **`electron exceed`** inside **`superelectron exceed`** do not false-positive. - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`orbitals exceed`** / **`orbitals exceeded`** and singular **`orbital exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`band exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`bands exceed`**, so batch / JSON / DFT / quantum-chemistry-style APIs that describe request **`orbitals`** still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`orbitals`** / **`orbital`** so **`microorbitals exceed`**, **`metaorbitals exceed`**, **`suborbital exceed`**, **`preorbital exceed`**, **`reorbital exceed`**, and embedded **`orbital exceed`** inside **`superorbital exceed`** do not false-positive. - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`primitive cells exceed`** / **`primitive cells exceeded`** and singular **`primitive cell exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`unit cell exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`unit cells exceed`**, so batch / JSON / crystallography or lattice-style APIs that describe request **`primitive cells`** still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary at **`primitive`** so **`microprimitivecells exceed`**, **`metaprimitivecells exceed`**, **`subprimitivecell exceed`**, **`preprimitivecell exceed`**, **`reprimitivecell exceed`**, and embedded **`primitive cell exceed`** inside **`superprimitivecell exceed`** do not false-positive (no space inside **`primitivecells`**, so the contiguous phrase **`primitive cells exceed`** is absent there; a spaced **`micro primitive cells …`** still matches at the boundary before **`primitive`**). HTTP rate limits, per-basis / Wigner–Seitz caps, and other **`primitive cells exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D441.)

## [0.1.58] - 2026-03-24

### Added
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`skyrmions exceed`** / **`skyrmions exceeded`** and singular **`skyrmion exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`instanton exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`instantons exceed`**, so batch / JSON / magnetism or topological-defect-style APIs that describe request **`skyrmions`** still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so **`microskyrmions exceed`**, **`metaskyrmions exceed`**, **`subskyrmion exceed`**, **`preskyrmion exceed`**, **`reskyrmion exceed`**, and embedded **`skyrmion exceed`** inside **`superskyrmion exceed`** do not false-positive. HTTP rate limits, per-track / topological-charge caps, and other **`skyrmions exceed`** lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D423.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`instantons exceed`** / **`instantons exceeded`** and singular **`instanton exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`soliton exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`solitons exceed`**, so batch / JSON / gauge-theory or tunneling-style APIs that describe request **`instantons`** still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so **`microinstantons exceed`**, **`metainstantons exceed`**, **`subinstanton exceed`**, **`preinstanton exceed`**, **`reinstanton exceed`**, and embedded **`instanton exceed`** inside **`superinstanton exceed`** do not false-positive. - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`solitons exceed`** / **`solitons exceeded`** and singular **`soliton exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`plasmon exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`plasmons exceed`**, so batch / JSON / nonlinear-optics or pulse-style APIs that describe request **`solitons`** still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so **`microsolitons exceed`**, **`metasolitons exceed`**, **`subsoliton exceed`**, **`presoliton exceed`**, **`resoliton exceed`**, and embedded **`soliton exceed`** inside **`supersoliton exceed`** do not false-positive. - **Browser tools: forward, reload, and keyboard chords** — **`BROWSER_GO_FORWARD`** (one history step forward in the focused tab, same semantics as **`BROWSER_GO_BACK`**), **`BROWSER_RELOAD`** (CDP `Page.reload`; optional **`nocache`** / **`hard`** / **`bypass`** for cache-bypass), and **`BROWSER_KEYS`** (allowlisted CDP key chords to the **page** only via `Input.dispatchKeyEvent`; **`+`**-joined modifiers + key, e.g. `Meta+f`, `Escape`; no HTTP fallback). Wired through `browser_tool_dispatch`, `tool_loop` (sequence-terminating for navigate/back/forward/reload like existing navigation tools), `tool_parsing`, and agent prompts. (`browser_agent/mod.rs`, `commands/browser_tool_dispatch.rs`, `tool_loop.rs`, `tool_parsing.rs`, `agent_descriptions.rs`, `config/mod.rs`; `docs/029_browser_automation.md`, `docs/agent_workflow.md`.)

- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses **`contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary`** for the FEAT-D295-guarded **`message`/`messages`/`input`/`inputs` … `too long`** phrases (same explicit context-slot list as **`messages exceed`**), replacing substring **`contains`** on that conjunct so embedded forms like **`message is too long`** inside **`submessage is too long`** are not counted at that arm (FEAT-D391; unit test **`message_input_too_long_phrases_use_ident_boundary_on_conjunct`**). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses **`contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary`** on bounded JSON-key overflow disjuncts (**`n_ctx`**, **`num_ctx`**, **`max_context`** / camelCase / snake_case / **`n_ctx_per_seq`**), word-order anchors (**`maximum context`**, **`max context`**, **`maximum allowed context`**, **`max allowed context`**, **`context length limit`**) and their verb OR-lists, and on FEAT-D309–D319 **`calls`/`batches`/`items`/`entries`/`chunks`/`documents`/`files`/`lines`/`cells` exceed** arms (same explicit context-slot guard as **`messages exceed`**), so embedded **`micro…`** / **`meta…`** forms and **`microexceed`**-style compounds no longer false-positive (FEAT-D390). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses helpers **`explicit_context_slot_after_ident_boundary`** and **`token_overflow_slot_conjunct_after_ident_boundary`** so the FEAT-D295 explicit context-slot OR list (**`context window`**, **`max context`**, **`model's context`**, etc.) and the loose slot under **`total tokens exceed`** / **`prompt`**/**`input tokens exceed`** no longer use plain **`contains`**, avoiding false positives when those substrings sit inside compounds like **`microcontext window`** or **`microwindow`** (FEAT-D389). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` on compound arms (**`context budget`**, **`conversation`** + **`too long`** + **`context`**, **`too long`** / **`too large`** / fit phrasing + **`context`**, **`context buffer`** / **`configured context`** / capacity / allocation, **`would exceed`** + **`context`**, **`truncated`** + context slots, **`context`** + exhausted wording, **`kv cache`** + **`is full`** + **`context`**, **`context window`** + **`too small`**, **`prefill`** + **`context`**) so a bare **`contains("context")`** match inside **`microcontext`** no longer satisfies those conjuncts (FEAT-D388). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for fixed prose phrases including **`context size exceeded`**, **`exceeds available context`**, limit / size / **`exceed the maximum context`** / token-limit wording, and demonstrative **`exceeds` / `exceeded` / `exceed this model's context`**, so the same substrings embedded after an ASCII ident continuation (e.g. **`microcontext size exceeded`**, **`micropast the context`**, **`microcontext exhausted`**) no longer match (FEAT-D387). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for **`requested more tokens than`**, **`fit in the context`**, **`larger than the context`**, preposition + **`context window`** phrases (**`outside`** / **`beyond`** / **`over`**, with optional **`the`**), compact **`outside` / `beyond` / `over` + `context window`**, **`beyond the context`**, and **`ran out of context`** / **`running out of context`**, so the same substrings embedded after an ASCII ident continuation (e.g. **`microrequested more tokens than`**, **`microfit in the context`**, **`microbeyond the context window`**, **`microran out of context`**) no longer match (FEAT-D386). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for **`exceeds the model's context window`**, parallel **`model context`** / **`model's maximum context`** **`exceed*`** phrases, **`exceeds the context window`**, **`context window exceeded`**, and **`exceeded` / `exceeds` / `exceed the context limit`**, so the same substrings embedded after an ASCII ident continuation (e.g. **`microexceeds the model's context window`**, **`micromodel context exceeded`**) no longer match (FEAT-D385). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for **`context overflow`**, **`context length exceeded`**, and **`maximum context length`**, so the same substrings embedded inside **`microcontext …`** / **`micromaximum context length`** no longer match (FEAT-D384). - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for **`prompt too long`**, **`prompt is too long`**, **`prompt has more tokens than`**, and **`prompt exceeds the context`**, so the same substrings embedded inside **`microprompt …`** forms no longer match (FEAT-D383). - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for **`input sequence is too long`** and **`prompt length exceeds`**, so embedded **`input sequence is too long`** inside **`microinput sequence is too long`** and **`prompt length exceeds`** inside **`microprompt length exceeds`** no longer match (FEAT-D382). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for plural **`queries exceed`** / **`queries exceeded`** and singular **`query exceed`** (same context-slot guard as **`requests exceed`** / **`inputs exceed`**), so embedded **`queries exceed`** inside **`microqueries exceed`** / **`metaqueries exceed`** and **`query exceed`** inside **`subquery exceed`** / **`prequery exceed`** / **`requery exceed`** no longer match with a context slot (FEAT-D380). - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for plural **`contents exceed`** / **`contents exceeded`** and singular **`content exceed`** (same context-slot guard as **`inputs exceed`** / **`outputs exceed`**), so embedded **`contents exceed`** inside **`microcontents exceed`** / **`metacontents exceed`** and **`content exceed`** inside **`subcontent exceed`** / **`precontent exceed`** / **`recontent exceed`** no longer match with a context slot (FEAT-D379). - **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for plural **`responses exceed`** / **`responses exceeded`** and singular **`response exceed`** (same context-slot guard as **`outputs exceed`**), so embedded **`responses exceed`** inside **`microresponses exceed`** / **`metaresponses exceed`** and **`response exceed`** inside **`subresponse exceed`** / **`preresponse exceed`** / **`reresponse exceed`** no longer match with a context slot (FEAT-D378). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` (FEAT-D377): ident-boundary on **`total prompt tokens exceed`**, **`requested tokens exceed`**, guarded **`total tokens exceed`**, and guarded **`input tokens exceed`**. **`prompt tokens exceed`** uses ident-boundary plus skipping when the preceding ASCII ident token is a compound ending in **`total`** (via **`preceding_ascii_ident_token`**). The FEAT-D311 **`tokens exceed`** / **`tokens exceeded`** arm uses the same boundary helper and skips when the prior token ends with **`prompt`**, **`input`**, **`total`**, or **`requested`**, so lines like **`micrototal prompt tokens exceed`** and **`microrequested tokens exceed`** do not match on the generic **`tokens exceed`** path. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for plural **`outputs exceed`** / **`outputs exceeded`** and singular **`output exceed`** (same context-slot guard as **`inputs exceed`**), so embedded **`outputs exceed`** inside **`microoutputs exceed`** / **`metaoutputs exceed`** and **`output exceed`** inside **`suboutput exceed`** / **`preoutput exceed`** / **`reoutput exceed`** no longer match with a context slot (FEAT-D376). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` uses `contains_phrase_after_ident_boundary` for plural **`inputs exceed`** / **`inputs exceeded`** and singular **`input exceed`** (same context-slot guard as **`messages exceed`**), so embedded **`inputs exceed`** inside **`microinputs exceed`** / **`metainputs exceed`** and **`input exceed`** inside **`subinput exceed`** / **`preinput exceed`** / **`reinput exceed`** no longer match with a context slot (FEAT-D375). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Browser agent (CDP)** — When Chrome is connected but has **no open page tabs**, the agent creates one **`about:blank`** tab, brings it forward, updates the focused tab index, and registers the dialog auto-dismiss hook so **BROWSER_NAVIGATE** / **BROWSER_CLICK** / etc. recover without a manual tab. Failure logs at **warn** and returns a clear error. (`browser_agent/mod.rs`, `docs/029_browser_automation.md`.)
- **Browser agent (CDP)** — **`/json/version`** discovery uses short per-request HTTP timeouts with **retries** so a flaky probe does not immediately fall through to launching Chrome; after WebSocket connect, **polls until tab listing succeeds** with at least one tab (bounded wait) before treating the session as ready. Session reuse skips the readiness poll; docs describe default **5-minute** CDP idle timeout (`browserIdleTimeoutSecs`). (`browser_agent/mod.rs`, `docs/029_browser_automation.md`.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural **`probabilities exceed`** / **`probabilities exceeded`** and singular **`probability exceed`** (present/past via the same **`exceed`** prefix as **`logit exceed`**) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as **`messages exceed`** / **`logits exceed`**, with ASCII alnum/`_` left-boundary guards (FEAT-D373). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`.)
- **Agent workflow docs** — OpenClaw reviewer re-run timestamp (`005-openclaw-reviewer/005-openclaw-reviewer.md`); FEATURE-CODER backlog and “When empty” through FEAT-D423 (`006-feature-coder/FEATURE-CODER.md`); closing reviewer entry point (`004-closing-reviewer/CLOSING-REVIEWER-PROMPT.md`); closing reviewer smoke-test checklist for FEAT-D389–D423 (`docs/022_feature_review_plan.md`).

## [0.1.55] - 2026-03-22

### Added
- **Downloads organizer** — Moves top-level files in `~/Downloads` (or a configured path) into subfolders using markdown rules (`~/.mac-stats/agents/downloads-organizer-rules.md`); ships default rules; Tauri commands and dashboard settings; background check every 60s when enabled (`hourly` / `daily` / `off`, dry-run default). (`downloads_organizer/`, `commands/downloads_organizer.rs`, `config/mod.rs`, `lib.rs`, `dashboard.html` / `dashboard.js`, `docs/024_downloads_organizer.md`.)

### Changed
- **Browser agent (CDP)** — Clearer navigation failures: detects `chrome-error://` after navigate, skips cookie-banner logic on error documents, logs host-only + compact error class, sanitizes errors for tools/LLM (path redaction, length cap). (`browser_agent/mod.rs`, `http_fallback.rs`.)
- **Server-side fetch** — `fetch_page_post_form_urlencoded` for `application/x-www-form-urlencoded` POST with the same SSRF, redirect, timeout, and body truncation as GET. Optional homoglyph normalization for untrusted page text via `normalizeUntrustedHomoglyphs` / `MAC_STATS_NORMALIZE_UNTRUSTED_HOMOGLYPHS`. (`commands/browser.rs`, `commands/text_normalize.rs`, tool dispatch paths, `config/mod.rs`.)

## [0.1.56] - 2026-03-23

### Changed
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural `metrics exceed` / `metrics exceeded` and singular `metric exceed` (present/past via the same `exceed` prefix as `resource exceed`) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as `messages exceed` / `resources exceed`, so observability or batch APIs that describe request `metrics` still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so `micrometrics exceed`, `metametrics exceed`, and `submetric exceed` do not false-positive, and `premetric exceed` / `remetric exceed` do not match embedded `metric exceed`. HTTP rate limits, cardinality or series caps, and other `metrics exceed` lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D361.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural `resources exceed` / `resources exceeded` and singular `resource exceed` (present/past via the same `exceed` prefix as `scope exceed`) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as `messages exceed` / `scopes exceed`, so OpenTelemetry-style Resource or batch APIs that describe `resources` still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so `microresources exceed`, `metaresources exceed`, and `subresource exceed` do not false-positive, and `preresource exceed` / `reresource exceed` do not match embedded `resource exceed`. HTTP rate limits, per-resource attribute caps, and other `resources exceed` lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D360.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural `scopes exceed` / `scopes exceeded` and singular `scope exceed` (present/past via the same `exceed` prefix as `link exceed`) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as `messages exceed` / `links exceed`, so OpenTelemetry-style instrumentation-scope or batch APIs that describe `scopes` still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so `microscopes exceed`, `metascopes exceed`, and `subscope exceed` do not false-positive, and `prescope exceed` / `rescope exceed` do not match embedded `scope exceed`. HTTP rate limits, per-scope attribute caps, and other `scopes exceed` lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D359.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural `packets exceed` / `packets exceeded` and singular `packet exceed` (present/past via the same `exceed` prefix as `fragment exceed`) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as `messages exceed` / `fragments exceed`, so streaming or datagram APIs that describe request `packets` still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so compounds like `micropackets exceed`, `metapackets exceed`, and `subpacket exceed` do not false-positive, and `repacket exceed` does not match embedded `packet exceed`. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D304.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural `contents exceed` / `contents exceeded` and singular `content exceed` (present/past via the same `exceed` prefix as `message exceed`) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as `messages exceed` / `inputs exceed`, so batch APIs that describe payload `contents` still map to the overflow message; substring `content exceed` does not match plural `contents exceed`; attachment sizing and rate-limit lines without slot wording stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D303.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural `inputs are too long` and `inputs were too long` when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as `messages are too long` / singular `input is/was too long` (FEAT-D296), so batch APIs that describe multiple payloads in the plural still map to the overflow message; generic form or UI limits without those phrases stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D302.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` treats possessive `model's context` as an explicit context-slot phrase alongside `context window` / `max context` / `available context` for the same guarded arms as FEAT-D295 (`messages exceed`, singular `message exceed(s/ed)`, `inputs exceed`, `input exceed`, and guarded `message`/`input` + `too long`), so lines like “your message is too long for this model's context” map to the overflow message; bare `model context` in unrelated copy (e.g. “no model context configured”) still does not match those arms. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D301.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes singular `input exceed` / `exceeds` / `exceeded` when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as plural `inputs exceed` (substring `input exceed` does not match `inputs exceed`), so one-shot request errors still map to the overflow message; rate limits, attachment sizing, and other lines without those phrases stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D300.)

- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes `message is too long`, `messages are too long`, past-tense `message was` / `messages were`, and `input is` / `input was too long` when paired with the same explicit context-slot wording as `messages exceed`, so chat/API errors that say “message too long” (not “prompt too long”) still map to the overflow message; generic character-limit lines without those phrases stay unmatched. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D296.)
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes `messages exceed` / `messages exceeded` when paired with explicit context-slot wording (`context window`, `context length`, `context limit`, `context size`, `max context`, `maximum context`, or `available context`), so chat-completions-style errors map to the same user-facing overflow message without matching unrelated lines that mention `messages exceed` and incidental `model context`. Snake/camel option keys that require overflow wording (`max_context`, `context_length`, `context_window`, `context_limit`, `maxcontext`, `contextlength`, `contextlimit`, `n_ctx_per_seq`, `n_ctx`, `num_ctx`) now use the same token boundaries so prefixed identifiers (e.g. `old_context_length_exceeded`) do not false-positive when `exceeded` contains `exceed`. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`; FEAT-D294.)

- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — `collapse_whitespace()` maps Latin Extended-D spacing `Sk` scalars U+A720 MODIFIER LETTER STRESS AND HIGH TONE, U+A721 STRESS AND LOW TONE, U+A789 MODIFIER LETTER COLON, and U+A78A MODIFIER LETTER SHORT EQUALS SIGN to ASCII space; not Rust whitespace—phonetic or Unicode-sample HTML can otherwise glue Latin tokens. Block letters (`Lu`/`Ll`) and U+A788 MODIFIER LETTER LOW CIRCUMFLEX ACCENT (`Lm`) stay unmapped. Tests `latin_extended_d_modifier_letters_sk_a720_a721_a789_a78a_separate_words`, `latin_extended_d_modifier_letter_lm_a788_and_letter_ll_a723_stay_unmapped` in `commands/html_cleaning.rs`. (FEAT-D241.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — `collapse_whitespace()` no longer maps U+02C6 MODIFIER LETTER CIRCUMFLEX ACCENT and U+02C7 CARON: UnicodeData classifies them as `Lm`, not `Sk`, so FEAT-D239’s `U+02C2..=U+02C7` arm split IPA-style superscript diacritics incorrectly. Arrowhead word separators remain `U+02C2..=U+02C5`. Tests `spacing_modifier_arrowheads_sk_u02c2_through_u02c5_and_tacks_u02d2_through_u02d5_separate_words`, `spacing_modifier_circumflex_and_caron_lm_u02c6_u02c7_stay_unmapped` in `commands/html_cleaning.rs`. (FEAT-D240.)
- **HTML cleaning (comments only)** — `collapse_whitespace` and `mongolian_punctuation_separate_words` now name U+1806 as **MONGOLIAN TODO SOFT HYPHEN** so the Unicode-standard substring `TODO` is not read as a developer TODO. No tokenizer change. (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`; FEAT-D219.)

### Fixed
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Removed `collapse_whitespace()` mapping for U+10D29–U+10D2D: current UnicodeData leaves U+10D28–U+10D2F unassigned (`Cn`) between U+10D27 (`Mn`) and Hanifi digits U+10D30+ (`Nd`); the old arm matched stale Hanifi Rohingya sentence `Po` assignments (historical FEAT-D111). Tests `hanifi_rohingya_unassigned_gap_u10d28_through_u10d2f_stays_unmapped`, `hanifi_rohingya_combining_signs_mn_u10d24_through_u10d27_stay_unmapped`, `hanifi_rohingya_digit_nd_u10d30_stays_unmapped` in `commands/html_cleaning.rs`. (FEAT-D254.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Removed `collapse_whitespace()` mapping for U+1734 **HANUNOO SIGN PAMUDPOD**: UnicodeData classifies it as `Mn`, not Philippine sentence `Po`; FEAT-D83’s `U+1734..=U+1736` arm incorrectly folded a combining mark into word separators. **PHILIPPINE SINGLE PUNCTUATION** U+1735 and **PHILIPPINE DOUBLE PUNCTUATION** U+1736 remain mapped. Tests `philippine_single_double_punctuation_separate_words`, `hanunoo_sign_pamudpod_mn_u1734_stays_unmapped` in `commands/html_cleaning.rs`. (FEAT-D253.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Removed `collapse_whitespace()` mapping for U+213F: UnicodeData assigns **DOUBLE-STRUCK CAPITAL PI** (`Lu`), not n-ary summation; **DOUBLE-STRUCK N-ARY SUMMATION** is U+2140 (`Sm`), which remains a word separator with U+2141–U+2144. Historical FEAT-D231 / changelog text assumed the wrong code point. Tests `letterlike_symbol_subranges_separate_words`, `letterlike_mathematical_letters_stay_unmapped` in `commands/html_cleaning.rs`. (FEAT-D246.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Removed `collapse_whitespace()` mapping for U+AAF2 **MEETEI MAYEK ANJI**: UnicodeData classifies it as `Lo`, not `Po`, so the FEAT-D218 arm split Meetei script text incorrectly. U+AAF0–U+AAF1 (`Po`) remain word separators; test `meetei_mayek_anji_lo_u_aaf2_stays_unmapped` in `commands/html_cleaning.rs`. (FEAT-D221.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Removed `collapse_whitespace()` mapping for U+1057B–U+1057F: current UnicodeData leaves U+1057B unassigned (`Cn`) and assigns U+1057C–U+1057F as Vithkuqi capital letters (`Lu`), not sentence punctuation, so the old arm split script text incorrectly (historical FEAT-D117 mismatch). Caucasian Albanian citation mark U+1056F (`Po`) unchanged. Test `vithkuqi_capital_letters_and_gap_u1057b_stay_unmapped` in `commands/html_cleaning.rs`. (FEAT-D220.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Wancho arm narrowed to U+1E2FF only: current UnicodeData places Wancho digits at U+1E2F0–U+1E2F9 (`Nd`), leaves U+1E2FA–U+1E2FE unassigned (`Cn`), and assigns WANCHO NGUN SIGN at U+1E2FF (`Sc`). The old `U+1E2FE..=U+1E2FF` range matched stale “comma / full stop (`Po`)” copy and mapped non-characters; digits and the gap stay unmapped, Ngün remains a word separator. (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`; FEAT-D214; historical FEAT-D91 Wancho note.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Removed `collapse_whitespace()` mapping for U+10FF5: Unicode classifies it as Elymaic letter taw (`Lo`), not punctuation, so treating it as a word separator broke Elymaic text (historical FEAT-D110 mismatch). Nabataean / Hatran / Old North Arabian `Po` separators unchanged. (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`; FEAT-D213.)
- **HTML cleaning (FETCH_URL)** — Removed `collapse_whitespace()` mapping for U+118C8–U+118CF: Unicode 14+ classifies them as Warang Citi small letters (`Ll`), not sentence punctuation, so treating them as word separators broke Warang Citi text. Hanifi Rohingya U+10D29–U+10D2D was removed separately once UnicodeData left that range unassigned (**FEAT-D254** in this release). (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`; FEAT-D212.)

- **HTML cleaning: bidi / CGJ / isolates (FETCH_URL)** — `collapse_whitespace()` maps U+034F (combining grapheme joiner), U+061C (Arabic letter mark), U+200E/U+200F (LRM/RLM), and U+2066–U+2069 (directional isolates) to a normal space before tokenizing, same family as ZWSP/ZWNJ: Rust’s `split_whitespace()` does not treat those code points as whitespace, so without mapping, `hello\u{200E}world` (and similar) would stay one token. (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`; `nbsp_separates_words` test; FEAT-D35.)
- **HTML cleaning: soft hyphen word breaks (FETCH_URL)** — `collapse_whitespace()` maps U+00AD (soft hyphen, common from HTML `&shy;`) to a normal space before tokenizing, same family as ZWSP/BOM: Rust’s `split_whitespace()` does not treat SHY as whitespace, so without mapping, `hello\u{00AD}world` would stay one token. (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`; `soft_hyphen_separates_words` test; FEAT-D34.)
- **HTML cleaning: zero-width word breaks (FETCH_URL)** — `collapse_whitespace()` maps U+200B (ZWSP) and U+FEFF (BOM as ZWNBSP when it appears in text) to a normal space before tokenizing, so glued tokens like `hello\u{200B}world` become `hello world` for the model. Rust’s `split_whitespace()` does not treat those code points as whitespace. (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`; `zero_width_space_separates_words` test; FEAT-D33.)
- **`load_agents` shared-soul log (022 §F3)** — `info!` line for shared `soul.md` presence now runs whenever `load_agents` finishes a scan: agents dir missing, no enabled agents, or successful load (previously only when at least one agent was enabled). Pure helper `shared_soul_file_nonempty()` + `log_shared_soul_presence()`; three HOME-override unit tests. (`agents/mod.rs`; FEAT-D27.)
- **CPU window chat: reserved words (022 §F8)** — `--cpu` and `-v`/`-vv`/`-vvv` are handled before any user chat bubble is added, so meta-commands stay out of the visible transcript as well as conversation history. Input is cleared immediately; only the assistant status line is shown. (`src/ollama.js`, synced to `src-tauri/dist/ollama.js`; FEAT-D16.)
- **Agent-router execution messages (022 §F2)** — Both execution paths in `answer_with_ollama_and_fetch` now use `build_execution_message_stack()` (`session_history.rs`) for system → history → current user; two unit tests lock the ordering contract. No change to wire format or model payloads. (`commands/session_history.rs`, `commands/ollama.rs`)
- **TASK agent paragraph helper** — **TASK** block in `build_agent_descriptions` moved to `format_task_agent_description()` for unit testing; wording unchanged. (`commands/agent_descriptions.rs`)

### Documentation
- **FEATURE-CODER backlog (FEAT-D68–D76)** — Table rows for Small Form Variants + CJK compatibility punctuation (U+FE50–U+FE6B ranges, U+3030 / U+3037 / U+303D / U+30A0 / U+FF3F), Latin-1 / Greek question mark / Arabic script punctuation (U+00A1 / U+00BF / U+00AB / U+00BB / U+037E / U+060C / U+061B / U+061F / U+06D4 / U+066A–U+066C), Latin-1 section + pilcrow (U+00A7 / U+00B6), Armenian script punctuation (U+055C–U+055F, U+0589–U+058A), Hebrew sof pasuq + Georgian paragraph separator (U+05C3, U+10FB), CJK Symbols brackets / ditto / wave / vertical repeat / masu (U+3003–U+303F selective), Devanagari danda + double danda (U+0964–U+0965), Thai / Lao / Myanmar sentence punctuation (U+0E2F / U+0E4F / U+0E5A–U+0E5B / U+0EAF / U+104A–U+104B), and Tibetan shad stack / yig mgo / corner brackets / paluta / astrological marks (U+0F04–U+0F12, U+0F14, U+0F3A–U+0F3D, U+0F85, U+0FD0–U+0FD4, U+0FD9–U+0FDA). (`006-feature-coder/FEATURE-CODER.md`.)

(`006-feature-coder/FEATURE-CODER.md`.)
- **`toggle_cpu_window` from CPU window chat (022 §F8)** — Rustdoc clarifies that reserved word `--cpu` from inside the CPU window uses the same close-then-recreate path as the menu bar (WebView destroyed and recreated, not an in-place hide). `docs/022_feature_review_plan.md` F8 checklist item closed. (`commands/window.rs`, `ui/status_bar.rs`; FEAT-D31.)
- **`toggle_cpu_window` + `run_on_main_thread` (022 §F9)** — Rustdoc on `commands/window.rs` explains Tauri 1 threading: the command runs off the AppKit main thread, `run_on_main_thread` blocks the command thread until a short main-thread window close/create completes; checklist item in `docs/022_feature_review_plan.md` F9 marked complete. No runtime behaviour change. (FEAT-D30.)
- **`toggle_cpu_window` API docs (022 §F9)** — Rustdoc on `commands/window.rs` and `ui/status_bar.rs` matches implementation: existing CPU window is closed then recreated so the user always ends with a visible window; clarifies this is not a strict “close and stay closed” toggle. (FEAT-D29.)

- **README product overview** — New **What mac-stats ships with** section up front (menu bar metrics, Ollama toolbelt, Discord/tasks/scheduler/monitors, privacy/ops); trimmed duplicate “At a glance” bullets; cross-link to `docs/006_roadmap_ai_tasks.md`. **`docs/README.md`** Global Context now defers to root README; **`docs/006_roadmap_ai_tasks.md`** title clarifies roadmap vs product overview.
- **022 feature review checklist** — Per-section review items in `docs/022_feature_review_plan.md` marked complete where automated tests or code paths already cover them (F1–F4, F6, F7, F8, F10); integration table updated for session file compat and `run_due_monitor_checks` caller. Manual Discord/smoke rows unchanged. (FEAT-D26.)
- **Autoresearch snapshot plotter** — `scripts/plot_autoresearch_snapshot.py` reads mac-stats-reviewer Track A `results.tsv` and writes PNG/SVG (optional `state.json` subtitle). Generate outputs locally when needed; large samples are not kept in-tree.
- **022 review & FEATURE-CODER backlog** — F5 checklist items marked complete with test pointers; new FEAT-D9–D11 rows in the coder backlog. (`docs/022_feature_review_plan.md`, `006-feature-coder/FEATURE-CODER.md`)

### Removed
- **Autoresearch sample artifacts** — Dropped checked-in `docs/autoresearch-snapshots/amvara8-005-openclaw-24h_*` PNG/SVG/TSV/state JSON (~2.4k lines + binary) to reduce repo weight; recreate with `scripts/plot_autoresearch_snapshot.py` if you want the same plots.

### Fixed
- **Clippy `assertions_on_constants` (`prepare_conversation_history` tests)** — The below-threshold tokio tests no longer use runtime `assert!` on `COMPACTION_THRESHOLD`; a single `const` assert (`COMPACTION_THRESHOLD > 2`) in the test module documents the assumption (FEAT-D25). No runtime behaviour change. (`commands/session_history.rs`)
- **Clippy `assertions_on_constants` (session history caps)** — Ordering `HAVING_FUN_IDLE_HISTORY_CAP` < `CONVERSATION_HISTORY_CAP` is now a module-level `const` assert; the unit test only checks the literal values (20 / 10). (`commands/session_history.rs`; FEAT-D20.)
- **Monitor stats persistence after each check** — `check_monitor` now calls `save_monitors()` after updating `last_check` / `last_status`, so background `run_due_monitor_checks` and manual checks write `monitors.json` instead of keeping stats only in memory until add/remove. The monitors mutex is released before save to avoid deadlock with `save_monitors`’ lock order. Failures from `save_monitors` (e.g. busy `try_lock`) are ignored; in-memory stats remain authoritative for the running process. (`commands/monitors.rs`; FEAT-E1, 022 §3 F10.)

## [0.1.57] - 2026-03-23

### Changed
- **Ollama errors** — `is_context_overflow_error` recognizes plural `logits exceed` / `logits exceeded` and singular `logit exceed` (present/past via the same `exceed` prefix as `embedding exceed`) when paired with the same explicit context-slot phrases as `messages exceed` / `embeddings exceed`, so batched-inference / LM-head or batch APIs that describe request `logits` still map to the overflow message; phrases require an ASCII alnum/`_` left boundary so `micrologits exceed`, `metalogits exceed`, and `sublogit exceed` do not false-positive, and `prelogit exceed` / `relogit exceed` do not match embedded `logit exceed`. ## [0.1.54] - 2026-03-22

### Added
- **`cap_tail_chronological`** — Shared “last N items, chronological order” helper for conversation caps (agent router + Discord having_fun); unit tests lock the `rev().take(N).rev()` contract. Session memory test documents loading prior turns before recording the current user message (Discord pipeline). (`commands/session_history.rs`, `commands/ollama.rs`, `discord/mod.rs`, `session_memory.rs`)

### Changed
- **FETCH_URL oversized body** — When the response exceeds the char cap, the ellipsed text now ends with ` [content truncated]` (after reserving suffix length inside the cap) so the model explicitly knows content was cut, not only middle `...`. (`commands/browser.rs`)
- **`logging/subsystem.rs` test placement** — `#[cfg(test)] mod tests` now follows the exported `mac_stats_*` macros so `cargo clippy` stays warning-free (`items_after_test_module`). (`logging/subsystem.rs`)
- **Tracing targets** — Broad use of `mac_stats_*!` subsystem macros across agent commands, Discord, browser agent, MCP, plugins, scheduler, alerts, and related modules so logs align with `MAC_STATS_LOG` filtering.

### Fixed
- **Session resume: `## ` inside message body** — Persisted session markdown is parsed line-by-line; only lines that trim to exactly `## User` or `## Assistant` start a new turn. In-message text such as `## Notes` no longer splits the file incorrectly (previously `\n## ` truncation could drop content). Four unit tests. (`session_memory.rs`)
- **Website monitor `check_interval_secs = 0`** — Interval is clamped to at least 1 second when loading from disk, adding a monitor, and when deciding if a monitor is due in `run_due_monitor_checks`. Zero previously made `elapsed >= interval` true even with zero elapsed seconds after a check, so a monitor could be treated as due on every pass. (`commands/monitors.rs`)
- **SSRF redirect validation** — HTTP redirect targets are checked with the same rigor as the initial URL: DNS resolution failure or an empty address list stops the redirect instead of following blindly (extracted `check_redirect_target_ssrf`, used by `ssrf_redirect_policy`). Four new unit tests. (`commands/browser.rs`)
- **SSRF IPv4-mapped broadcast** — IPv6 addresses that embed IPv4 (e.g. `::ffff:255.255.255.255`) now treat mapped IPv4 broadcast the same as native IPv4 (`is_broadcast()` in the `to_ipv4_mapped()` guard). Unit test added. (`commands/browser.rs`)
- **Session resume after restart (legacy filenames)** — `load_messages_from_latest_session_file` now picks up both the current layout `session-memory-{id}-{timestamp}-{topic}.md` and the older `session-memory-{topic}-{id}-{timestamp}.md` files, so Discord/session context can load after upgrading from pre-reorder naming. Filename matching uses explicit new/legacy patterns (with unit tests) instead of a simple `session-memory-{id}-` prefix. (`session_memory.rs`)

## [0.1.53] - 2026-03-22

### Added
- **Discord draft message while tools run** — Full agent router posts a placeholder (“Processing…”), then throttled in-place edits (e.g. `Running FETCH_URL…`) until the final reply; the first chunk replaces the placeholder, extra chunks use new messages as before. Config `discord_draft_throttle_ms` or env `MAC_STATS_DISCORD_DRAFT_THROTTLE_MS` (default 1500 ms, clamped 200–60_000). If the placeholder send fails, falls back to reply-only mode. (`discord/mod.rs`, `commands/discord_draft_stream.rs`, `commands/tool_loop.rs`, `commands/ollama.rs`, `config/mod.rs`, `docs/007_discord_agent.md`)
- **`MAC_STATS_LOG` stderr filter** — Comma-separated subsystem allowlist (e.g. `browser,ollama`); console shows only events whose `tracing` target is `mac_stats::<name>` or a child path. File log (`~/.mac-stats/debug.log`) is unchanged. (`logging/subsystem.rs`, `logging/mod.rs`, `docs/039_mac_stats_log_subsystems.md`)
- **Subsystem `tracing` targets** — Ollama HTTP client, agent-router chat logs, and browser agent (CDP + HTTP fallback) use `mac_stats_*!` macros so they participate in `MAC_STATS_LOG`. (`ollama/mod.rs`, `commands/ollama.rs`, `browser_agent/mod.rs`, `browser_agent/http_fallback.rs`)

### Changed
- **MCP stdio errors** — Tool failures append short troubleshooting hints (PATH, timeouts, init/tools errors) pointing to `docs/038_ori_mnemos_mcp.md`; “not configured” mentions `MCP_SERVER_STDIO`. (`misc_tool_dispatch.rs`)
- **Docs** — Ori Mnemos MCP setup (`docs/038_ori_mnemos_mcp.md`); log subsystems reference (`docs/039_mac_stats_log_subsystems.md`); MCP agent doc, agent index/workflow, `README.md`, and `agents.md` cross-links.

## [0.1.52] - 2026-03-22

### Added
- **DISCORD_API pre-routing** — Discord API requests now skip the LLM planning step when the user's intent is unambiguous and a Discord bot token is configured. Explicit prefix (`DISCORD_API: <path>`) always pre-routes. Keyword patterns: "list servers" / "show servers" / "my servers" / "what servers am i in" → `DISCORD_API: GET /users/@me/guilds` (direct API call, no guild context needed). "list channels" / "show channels" / "list channels in …" → `AGENT: discord-expert` (needs guild discovery). "list members" / "show members" / "who's in …" → `AGENT: discord-expert` (needs guild context). Multi-step requests ("and then …", "after that …") are excluded and go through normal LLM planning. 22 new tests; 292 total pass, zero clippy warnings. (`commands/pre_routing.rs`)
- **Context-overflow auto-recovery** — When the Ollama API returns a context-window overflow error during the agent router or tool loop, oversized tool-result messages are automatically truncated and the request is retried instead of failing immediately. `is_context_overflow_error()` detects overflow patterns; `truncate_oversized_tool_results()` cuts messages exceeding the configured limit at word boundaries with a `[truncated]` marker. Applied in both `answer_with_ollama_and_fetch` (first execution call) and `run_tool_loop` (follow-up calls). If retry also fails, returns a clear message suggesting a new topic or larger context model. 12 new tests (truncation, overflow detection, skip system prompt, multiple results). (`commands/content_reduction.rs`, `commands/ollama.rs`, `commands/tool_loop.rs`)
- **Context-overflow config options** — `contextOverflowTruncateEnabled` (bool, default true) controls whether overflow recovery is attempted; `contextOverflowMaxResultChars` (number, default 4096) sets the per-message truncation limit. Both configurable via config.json or env vars (`MAC_STATS_CTX_OVERFLOW_TRUNCATE`, `MAC_STATS_CTX_OVERFLOW_MAX_RESULT_CHARS`). (`config/mod.rs`)
- **Discord full-router message debounce** — Rapid full-agent-router messages in the same channel merge into one Ollama run after a quiet period (default **2000 ms** via `discord_debounce_ms` in `~/.mac-stats/config.json`, env `MAC_STATS_DISCORD_DEBOUNCE_MS`, clamped 0–60s). Per-channel overrides in `discord_channels.json`: `debounce_ms` or `immediate_ollama: true`. Bypass: attachments, `/` commands, session-reset phrases, vision payloads; having_fun unchanged. Queued batches discarded on app disconnect (logged). Refactor: `run_discord_ollama_router` extracted. (`discord/message_debounce.rs`, `discord/mod.rs`, `config/mod.rs`, `defaults/discord_channels.json`, `docs/007_discord_agent.md`)

### Changed
- **Refactor `truncate_at_boundary`** — Replaced manual counter with `enumerate()` and a `broke_early` flag for clarity. No behavioral change. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`)
- **Compaction context cap** — The CONTEXT section produced by the session compaction LLM is now hard-capped at 12 000 bytes (~3 000 tokens) to prevent a verbose summary from consuming too much of the 32 K–40 K context window. Truncation cuts at the last sentence boundary (`.` / `!` / `?`) within budget, appends `[summary truncated]`, and is logged at warn level. Uses `floor_char_boundary` for safe UTF-8 handling. 7 new `cap_context` tests (short, exact, sentence boundary, no boundary, preserves punctuation, multibyte UTF-8, emoji) and 6 new `parse_compaction_output` tests (basic, no lessons, lessons-none, no headers, mixed-case, empty). 13 new tests; compaction module fully covered. (`commands/compaction.rs`)
- **Planning history cap** — The LLM planning step now receives only the last N conversation messages (default 6, ~3 user/assistant turns) instead of the full session history (up to 20). This reduces noise from past tool outputs that can bias the planner toward AGENT when a direct tool would suffice. Configurable via `planningHistoryCap` in config.json or env `MAC_STATS_PLANNING_HISTORY_CAP` (0 disables planning history entirely; max 40). The full history is still sent to the execution step. When capping is applied, logged at info level. (`commands/ollama.rs`, `config/mod.rs`)
- **Unit tests for `ellipse()` utility** — 12 new tests for the `ellipse()` string truncation function (widely used in 30+ call sites for log/status messages): short/exact/long strings, Unicode support, edge cases (empty, zero/one/three max_len), result length invariant, odd/even splits. (`logging/mod.rs`)
- **Unit tests for `merge_prompt_content` and `paragraph_key`** — 12 new tests for the prompt merge logic used at startup to add new default paragraphs to user-customized prompts without overwriting edits: empty existing, identical content, missing block appended, user edits preserved, no duplicates, exact first-line key matching, whitespace tolerance, planning_history_cap default. (`config/mod.rs`)
- **HTML noise stripping for FETCH_URL** — Fetched page content is now cleaned before being sent to the LLM: `script`, `style`, `head`, `meta`, `link`, `noscript`, `svg`, `iframe`, `object`, and `embed` tags are stripped entirely. Semantic structure is preserved: headings as `# …`, links as `[text](href)`, list items as `- …`, table rows as pipe-separated values, and block elements as newlines. Typical pages shrink 40–70%, saving context tokens and often avoiding the summarization Ollama round-trip. When cleaning produces empty output (all-JS pages), a helpful message suggests BROWSER_NAVIGATE instead. Compression ratio logged at info level. Applied to FETCH_URL in Discord/agent tool loop and CPU-window chat; HTTP fallback (which needs raw HTML for its own parser) is unaffected. 11 new tests; 221 total pass, zero clippy warnings. (`commands/html_cleaning.rs`, `commands/network_tool_dispatch.rs`, `commands/ollama_frontend_chat.rs`)
- **Scheduler per-task wall-clock timeout** — Each scheduler task is now wrapped in `tokio::time::timeout` to prevent a single stuck task from blocking the scheduler loop indefinitely. Default 600 s (10 min), configurable via `schedulerTaskTimeoutSecs` in config.json or env `MAC_STATS_SCHEDULER_TASK_TIMEOUT_SECS` (clamped 30–3600). Timed-out tasks are logged at error level and reported as failures. (`config/mod.rs`, `scheduler/mod.rs`)
- **Management command pre-routing** — LIST_SCHEDULES, TASK_LIST, TASK_SHOW, and OLLAMA_API management commands now skip the LLM planning step when the user's intent is unambiguous. Explicit prefixes (`LIST_SCHEDULES:`, `TASK_LIST:`, `TASK_SHOW: <id>`, `OLLAMA_API: <action>`) always pre-route. Keyword patterns: "list schedules" / "show schedules" / "what's scheduled" → LIST_SCHEDULES; "list tasks" / "show tasks" / "tasks" / "open tasks" / "all tasks" → TASK_LIST; "show task <id>" → TASK_SHOW; "list models" / "show models" / "what models are installed" / "available models" → OLLAMA_API: list_models; "pull model <name>" → OLLAMA_API: pull; "unload model <name>" → OLLAMA_API: unload; "running models" / "what models are running" → OLLAMA_API: running. Multi-step requests ("and then …", "after that …") are excluded and go through normal LLM planning. 33 new tests; 210 total pass, zero clippy warnings. (`commands/pre_routing.rs`)
- **BRAVE_SEARCH / PERPLEXITY_SEARCH pre-routing** — Requests with clear web search intent now skip the LLM planning step and route directly to the configured search tool. Explicit prefixes (`BRAVE_SEARCH: <query>`, `PERPLEXITY_SEARCH: <query>`) always pre-route. Keyword patterns ("search for …", "google …", "look up …", "web search …", "search the web for …", "search online for …", "research …") detect search intent and route to BRAVE_SEARCH (default) or PERPLEXITY_SEARCH ("research …" prefers Perplexity when configured; falls back to Brave). Multi-step requests ("and then …", "send to …", browser actions) are excluded and go through normal LLM planning. Only routes when the respective API key is configured. 21 new tests for `extract_search_query`; 177 total pass, zero clippy warnings. (`commands/pre_routing.rs`)
- **User-friendly Ollama API errors** — Known failures (context overflow, message role ordering, corrupted tool history) map to short actionable text via `sanitize_ollama_error_for_user()`; applied when surfacing errors from `answer_with_ollama_and_fetch`, CPU/chat `ollama_chat_with_execution` / continue, and `run_tool_loop`. Unknown errors keep prior formatting. New unit tests. (`commands/content_reduction.rs`, `commands/ollama.rs`, `commands/ollama_frontend_chat.rs`, `commands/tool_loop.rs`)
- **Docs: OpenClaw §96 re-verification** — All §7 checks re-run against OpenClaw AGENTS.md (23.9 KB, last modified 2026-03-21) vs code (`005-openclaw-reviewer`). Persistent findings from §95 confirmed still present: (1) `src/provider-web.ts` does not exist (actual: `src/channel-web.ts`); (2) `src/telegram`, `src/discord`, `src/slack`, `src/signal`, `src/imessage`, `src/web` do not exist as top-level dirs — channel runtimes live under `src/plugins/runtime/` and `src/channels/`, extensions under `extensions/`; (3) `pnpm format` runs `oxfmt --write` not `--check` (format check is `pnpm format:check`); (4) Vitest branch coverage threshold is 55%, not 70% as AGENTS.md line 109 claims (lines/functions/statements are 70%). New findings: (5) `pnpm tsgo` has no `scripts` entry in `package.json` — it relies on `@typescript/native-preview` (v7.0.0-dev.20260317.1) providing a `tsgo` binary via `.bin`; `pnpm check` calls `pnpm tsgo` in its chain, which works after `pnpm install` but is not a declared script; AGENTS.md line 69 documents `pnpm tsgo` as a standalone command. (6) AGENTS.md line 71 says `pnpm format` is "oxfmt --check" but actual `pnpm format` is `oxfmt --write`; the check command is `pnpm format:check`. (7) 82 extension dirs under `extensions/` (was 80 at §95); `anthropic-vertex`, `chutes`, `fal` still lack dedicated English provider pages; `phone-control` and `thread-ownership` still only in zh-CN plugin list. (8) SSRF test coverage in OpenClaw has grown significantly: 54 `it()` cases in 7 dedicated `*ssrf*.test.ts` files, plus ~14 SSRF-labeled tests across 11 other files (~68 total). (9) Recent commits: Discord routed through plugin SDK, plugin split runtime state, Claude bundle commands, context compaction notification, Matrix agentId mention fix, webchat image persistence, GitHub Copilot dynamic model IDs. No code bugs found; discrepancies are documentation-only.

## [0.1.51] - 2026-03-21

### Added
- **FETCH_URL pre-routing** — Requests with clear fetch/read intent and a URL (e.g. "fetch https://example.com", "get the page at https://…", "summarize this url https://…", or explicit "FETCH_URL: <url>") now skip the LLM planning step and route directly to `FETCH_URL`. Browser/navigate/screenshot patterns are excluded (handled by existing pre-routes). 17 new tests; 156 total pass, zero clippy warnings. (`commands/pre_routing.rs`)
- **General tool loop guard** — `ToolLoopGuard` in `commands/loop_guard.rs` detects repeated tool invocations and cycles within a single agent-router request. Tracks all (tool, arg) calls: blocks the same exact call after 3 invocations and detects repeating patterns of length 2–4 (e.g. A→B→A→B). Complements existing per-tool dedup (browser, Discord API, RUN_CMD) with cross-tool cycle detection. Blocked calls return an instructive message to the model ("reply with DONE or try a different approach"). 10 new tests; 139 total pass, zero clippy warnings. (`commands/loop_guard.rs`, `commands/mod.rs`, `commands/ollama.rs`)
- **Auto-dismiss JS dialogs in CDP browser agent** — Registered a `PageJavascriptDialogOpening` event listener that automatically dismisses `alert`, `confirm`, `prompt`, and `beforeunload` dialogs on CDP tabs. Prevents the browser agent from hanging when a page triggers a JS dialog. Handler is idempotent (tracked per tab pointer in a global `HashSet`), clears on browser session reset. Applied on `get_current_tab`, new-tab navigation, and screenshot flows. (`browser_agent/mod.rs`)
- **`scripts/screenshot-url.sh`** — Standalone headless Chrome screenshot utility for quick URL captures outside the app. Saves PNGs to `~/.mac-stats/screenshots/`.
- **Discord 429 rate-limit handling** — All Discord HTTP calls (`discord_api_request`, `send_message_to_channel`, `send_message_to_channel_with_attachments`) now honour 429 responses: parse `Retry-After` from header or JSON body, wait that duration plus pseudo-random jitter (100–499 ms), and retry up to 3 times. Each 429 is logged at warn level. Shared helpers `wait_for_rate_limit`, `retry_after_from_headers`, `parse_retry_after`, `jitter_millis` in `discord/api.rs`; `discord_api_request` refactored from fixed-iteration loop to an open loop with separate connection-retry and rate-limit-retry counters. (`discord/api.rs`, `discord/mod.rs`, `docs/007_discord_agent.md`)

All call sites (Discord, CLI `run-ollama`, scheduler, task runner, verification retry) updated to use struct initialization with `..Default::default()`, making each call self-documenting and new parameters trivial to add. `OllamaRequest` re-exported from `lib.rs`. No behavioral changes; zero clippy warnings, 139 tests pass. (`commands/ollama.rs`, `discord/mod.rs`, `main.rs`, `scheduler/mod.rs`, `task/runner.rs`, `lib.rs`)

## [0.1.50] - 2026-03-21

### Added
- **SSRF protection for all server-side URL fetches and browser navigations** — All model-triggered HTTP requests (`FETCH_URL`) and CDP navigations (`BROWSER_NAVIGATE`, `BROWSER_SCREENSHOT`) are now validated against a blocklist before execution: loopback (127.0.0.0/8, ::1), RFC 1918 private (10/8, 172.16/12, 192.168/16), link-local (169.254.0.0/16, fe80::/10), cloud metadata (169.254.169.254), IPv6 unique-local (fc00::/7), unspecified, broadcast, and IPv4-mapped IPv6 variants are all blocked. URLs with embedded credentials (userinfo) are rejected. DNS resolution is checked against the blocklist (catches hostnames resolving to private IPs). HTTP redirects are validated per-hop via a custom reqwest redirect policy. Configurable allowlist via `ssrfAllowedHosts` in `~/.mac-stats/config.json`. 14 new tests. (`commands/browser.rs`, `browser_agent/mod.rs`, `config/mod.rs`)

### Changed
- **agents.md: uptime section** — Added "Keep mac-stats running (uptime)" section with LaunchAgent recipe, operator checklist, lightweight watchdog, and coding-agent discipline notes. Updated restart coding principle to reference the new section.
- **Docs: SSRF protection** — Documented blocked targets, userinfo rejection, DNS resolution check, redirect protection, and allowlist in `docs/029_browser_automation.md`.

## [0.1.49] - 2026-03-21

### Added
- **Tool budget warning / last-iteration guidance** — When the agent approaches its tool iteration cap, budget warnings and last-iteration guidance are injected into the conversation to encourage result consolidation instead of starting new tool chains that would be cut off. Configurable via `toolBudgetWarningRatio` in config.json or env `MAC_STATS_TOOL_BUDGET_WARNING_RATIO` (0.0–1.0, default 0.75; 0.0 or 1.0 disables). (`commands/ollama.rs`, `config/mod.rs`)
- **Sequence-terminating navigation** — After a page-changing browser action (`BROWSER_NAVIGATE`, `BROWSER_GO_BACK`) in a multi-tool turn, remaining browser tools are skipped because element indices are stale. Non-browser tools still execute. The model receives the new page state and plans new actions in the next turn. (`commands/ollama.rs`)
- **Judge hook for CLI `--run-ollama`** — `run_judge_if_enabled()` now runs after `--run-ollama` completions. (`main.rs`, `lib.rs`)
- **Redmine query utility scripts** — `scripts/redmine_query.py` (Python, grouped time entry reports by ticket and day) and `scripts/redmine_query.sh` (curl wrapper). Both read credentials from `.config.env`.

### Removed
- **CLAUDE.md deleted** — Standalone `CLAUDE.md` removed; all content consolidated into `agents.md` as the single project instructions file.
- **Cleanup: old agent definition files** — Removed `005-openclaw-reviewer/005-openclaw-reviewer.md` and `006-feature-coder/FEATURE-CODER.md` (agent definitions now live in `~/.mac-stats/agents/`).
- **Cleanup: stale release notes** — Removed `release_notes_0.1.18.md`.
- **Cleanup: repetitive testing sections in `docs/022_feature_review_plan.md`** — Trimmed ~460 lines of duplicate closing-reviewer smoke test logs (content preserved in git history).

### Changed
- **agents.md expanded** — Added audience note, project overview at a glance, build/run section, backend runtime and performance summary (why CPU stays low, key technical choices, development notes, testing/debugging quick commands), and version management section. Now the single authoritative instructions file for Cursor, Claude Code, and similar tools.

- **Docs: tool budget warning** — Documented in `007_discord_agent.md` §17 (config, behavior, disabling).
- **Docs: sequence-terminating navigation** — Documented in `029_browser_automation.md`.
